## License: unknown

.get('/:id', async (req, res) => {
  try {
    const post = await Post.findById(req.params.id);
    if (!post) return res.status(404).json({ message: 'Post not found' });
    res.json(post);
  } catch (error) {
    res.status(500).json({ message: error.message });
```

            value={title}

            id="content"
            value={content}
            onChange={(e) => setContent(e.target.value)}
            required
          />
        </div>

```
